    <script type="text/javascript">
    var activeAbs = {"62":{"c":"5","d":"95"},"77":{"d":"75","e":"10","f":"10","c":"5"}};
    
    function runAb(name) {
        if ( !activeAbs || !activeAbs[name] ) {
            return null;
        }
        try {
            var cookie_val = $.cookie("aboption");
            if (cookie_val) {
                cookie_val = decodeURIComponent(cookie_val);
            }
            var abOpt = jQuery.parseJSON(cookie_val);
        } catch (e) {}
        if ( abOpt &amp;&amp; abOpt[name] &amp;&amp; activeAbs[name][abOpt[name]] ) {
            return abOpt[name];
        }
        var currentOpt = generateAb(activeAbs[name]);
        if ( currentOpt ) {
            recordAB(abOpt, name, currentOpt);
        }
        return currentOpt;
    }

    function recordAB(abOpt, name, currentOpt) {
        if ( !abOpt ) {
            abOpt = {};
        } else {
            $.each(abOpt, function(opt, val) {
                if ( !activeAbs[opt] ) {
                    delete abOpt[opt];
                }
            });
        }
        abOpt[name] = currentOpt;
        $.cookie("aboption", JSON.stringify(abOpt), { path: '/', domain: '.emag.ro', expires: 30 });
        $.ajax({url: "/ablogger.php?name=" + name + "&amp;value=" + currentOpt + "&amp;source=www"});

    }

    function generateAb(distribution) {
        var limit = 0;
        var rnd = Math.floor(Math.random() * 100 + 1);
        var curOpt = lastOpt = null;
        $.each(distribution, function(opt, val) {
            lastOpt = opt;
            limit+= parseFloat(val);
            if ( rnd &lt;= limit ) {
                curOpt = opt;
                return false;
            }
        });
        if ( curOpt ) {
            return curOpt;
        } else {
            return lastOpt;
        }
    }

    $(document).ready(function(){
        runAb(53);
        runAb(62);
        runAb(66);
        runAb(57);
        runAb(69);
        runAb(74);
        runAb(77);
    });
</script>

<script>
    $(window).load(function() {
        if (typeof ABcreateCookie != 'function'){
            function ABcreateCookie(name, value, days) {
                var expires = "";
                if (days) {
                    var date = new Date();
                    date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                    expires = "; expires=" + date.toGMTString();
                }
                document.cookie = name + "=" + value + expires + "; domain=.emag.ro; path=/";
            }
        }
        if (typeof readCookie != 'function') {
            function readCookie(name) {
                var nameEQ = name + "=";
                var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
                for (var i = 0; i &lt; ca.length; i++) {
                    var c = ca[i];
                    while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1, c.length);
                    if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
                }
                return null;
            }
        }

        var abTestingVariants = {};

        var cookieABTestingId = '12';
        var cookieVariant = '';

        if ((cookieABTestingId.length) &amp;&amp; (cookieVariant.length)) {
            if (readCookie('E_ABTesting')) {
                try {
                    abTestingVariants = JSON.parse(readCookie('E_ABTesting'));
                } catch (e) {}
            }

            // write cookie and register variant allocation IF cookie is missing OR IF is different from backend cookie
            if (typeof abTestingVariants[cookieABTestingId] == 'undefined' || abTestingVariants[cookieABTestingId] !== cookieVariant) {
                abTestingVariants[cookieABTestingId] = cookieVariant;

                ABcreateCookie('E_ABTesting', JSON.stringify(abTestingVariants), 30);
                try {
                    $.ajax('/ablogger.php?name=12&amp;value=&amp;source=www');
                } catch (e) {}
            }
        }
    })
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
$(document).ready(function(){
    if($.browser.msie &amp;&amp; get_browser_version() &lt;=10){
        function parseProductHolders(element) {
            var $elements = [];
            var $next = element;
            var processed = 0, mh = 0, mhf = 0, mhs = 0, hbk= 0, maxh = 0, hh = 0;
            while (processed &lt;= 5 &amp;&amp; $next.is('.product-holder-grid')) {
                var h = $next.find('h2').css('max-height', 'none').height();
                if (h &gt; mh) mh = h;
                var hf = $next.find('.family-description, .family-description-none').height();
                if (hf &gt; mhf) mhf = hf;
                var hs = $next.find('.stare-disp-listing').css('height', 'auto').height();
                if (hs &gt; mhs) mhs = hs;
                hh = $next.find('.feedback-right-msg').css('height', 'auto').height();
                if ( hh &gt; hbk ){ maxh = hh; hbk = maxh;}
                $elements.push($next);
                processed++;
                $next = $next.next();
                if ($next.is('script')) {
                    $next = $next.next();
                }
            }

            for (var i = 0; i &lt; processed; i++) {
                $elements[i].find('h2').height(mh);
                $elements[i].find('.family-description, .family-description-none').height(mhf);
                $elements[i].find('.stare-disp-listing').height(mhs);
                $elements[i].find('.feedback-right-msg').css('height', maxh);
            }
        }
        $('.big-box.listing #products-holder .product-holder-grid, #page-content.pageSubAction_search .content-with-sidebar .product-holder-grid, #page-content.pageType_search #products-holder .product-holder-grid, .big-box.listing .product-holder-grid')
        .filter(function(i) { return i % 5 == 0;}).each(function() {
            if($(this).parents().eq(2).hasClass('no-results-box2')) {
                $(this).parents().eq(2).children('.results').each(function(i) {
                    $(this).find('.product-holder-grid').filter(function(i) { return i % 5 == 0;}).each(function() {
                        parseProductHolders($(this));
                    });
                });
            } else {
                parseProductHolders($(this));
            }
        });
    }

    if (typeof eUserInfo != 'undefined' &amp;&amp; eUserInfo.email &amp;&amp; document.querySelector('#search-email')) {
        document.querySelector('#search-email').value = eUserInfo.email;
    }
});
</script>

<script>
    $(document).ready(function () {
        $('#emg-pagination-products-per-page ul.emg-custom-select-list li').click(function(){
            var link = $(this).find('a');
            $(link).trigger('click');
        });

        $("#emg-pagination-products-per-page").each(function(){
            $(this).emgSimpleSelectBox();
        });

        $('#emg-pagination-products-per-page ul.emg-custom-select-list li a').not('emg-ignore-js').click(function(event){
            event.stopPropagation();
            var pc = $(this).data('input');

            // DO NOT REMOVE THIS LINE
            $.cookie('emg_prod_count', pc, {expires: 365, path: '/', domain: "emag.ro"});
            $.cookie('emg_prod_count_changed', 1, {expires: 365, path: '/', domain: "emag.ro"});
            // COOKIE MUST BE SET FROM JAVASCRIPT (BECAUSE VARNISH)
            var redirectUrl = UpdateQueryString('pc', pc);
            window.location.href = redirectUrl;
        });

    });

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function(){
        $('input[name=giftconfig]').click(function(){
            for (promo_id in gifts_promo[$(this).attr('data-productid')]) {
                $('input[data-promoid='+promo_id+']').val(gifts_promo[$(this).attr('data-productid')][promo_id][$(this).attr('data-giftid')]);
            }
        });

        $('.hidden-list').not(':visible').each(function(){
            $(this).parent().css('margin-bottom', '0px');
        });

        $('.toggle-hidden-list').click(function(event) {
            event.preventDefault();
            if ($('.hidden-list').is(':visible')) {
                // hideListItems($('.toggle-hidden-items'));
                $('.hidden-list').hide();
                $('.hidden-list').each(function(){
                    $(this).parent().css('margin-bottom', '0px');
                });
                $(this).text('+ mai multe categorii');
            }
            else {
                // showListItems($('.toggle-hidden-items'));
                $('.hidden-list').show();
                // $('.filter-list-title').show();
                $('.hidden-list').each(function(){
                    $(this).parent().css('margin-bottom', '');
                });
                $(this).text('- mai puține categorii');
            }
            return false;
        });

    });
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">


//  FEEDBACK FORM JS

    function validateEmail(email) {
        var emailReg = /^([\w-\.]+@([\w-]+\.)+[\w-]{2,4})?$/;

        return emailReg.test( email );
    }

    function sendFeedback(satisfied)
    {
        var domObj = $('.search-feedback .search-feedback-modal');
        if (domObj.length == 0){
            domObj = $('.noresults-search-feedback .search-feedback-modal');
        }

        var page = 0;
                    page = 1;
        
        if ( satisfied == 'yes' || (domObj.find('#search-details').val().trim() != '' &amp;&amp; validateEmail(domObj.find('#search-email').val()))) {
            var problem = 0;
            if ($('#search-problem').val() != '') {
                problem = $('#search-problem').val();
            }
            var category = 0;
            
            $.ajax({
                url: '/search-tools/feedback',
                type: 'POST',
                data: {
                    'fraze': 'iphone 7',
                    'page': page,
                    'satisfied': satisfied,
                    'problem': problem,
                    'details': domObj.find('#search-details').val(),
                    'email': domObj.find('#search-email').val(),
                    'category': category
                },
                complete: function() {
                    var noresults = false;
                                        if (noresults &amp;&amp; $('.no-results-box2').length &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; !($('.no-results-box2').hasClass('fallback'))) {
                        $('.feedback-form-div').slideUp();
                        $('.search-feedback-trigger .content').hide();
                        $('.search-feedback-trigger .thx').slideDown();
                        $('.search-feedback-trigger').slideDown('fast');
                        $('.search-feedback-modal #search-form').get(0).reset();
                        $('#search-problem').attr('selectedIndex',0);
                        $('.gui-form-control').find('#select2-search-problem-container').html($('#search-problem').data('placeholder'));
                        setTimeout(function() {
                            $('.search-feedback-trigger').slideUp();
                            $('.feedback-form-div').slideDown();
                        }, 5000);
                    } else {
                        if (satisfied == 'no') {
                            $('.feedback-form-div').slideUp('fast');
                            $('.search-feedback-trigger').slideDown('fast');
                            $('.search-feedback-trigger .thx').slideDown('fast');
                        } else {
                            $('.search-feedback-trigger .thx').slideDown('fast');
                        }
                        $('.search-feedback-modal #search-form').get(0).reset();
                        $('#search-problem').attr('selectedIndex',0);
                        $('.gui-form-control').find('#select2-search-problem-container').html($('#search-problem').data('placeholder'));
                    }
                }
            });
        }
        else if (domObj.find('#search-details').val().trim() == '' &amp;&amp; !validateEmail(domObj.find('#search-email').val())) {
            domObj.find('#search-details').attr('placeholder', 'Acest câmp este obligatoriu!');
            domObj.find('#search-details').addClass('error-field');
            domObj.find('#search-details').addClass('error-text');
            domObj.find('#search-email').addClass('error-field');
        } else {
            if (domObj.find('#search-details').val().trim() == '') {
                domObj.find('#search-details').attr('placeholder', 'Acest câmp este obligatoriu!');
                domObj.find('#search-details').addClass('error-field');
                domObj.find('#search-details').addClass('error-text');
            } else {
                domObj.find('#search-email').addClass('error-field');
            }
        }
    }

    $(document).ready(function(){
        $(".go-page-btn").click(function(){
            var is_search = 1;
            var page = parseInt($(".go-page").val()) &gt; 0 ? parseInt($(".go-page").val()):1;

            if(page &lt; 1) page = 1;

            page = "/p"+page;
            if (is_search == 0) {
                if (from == 'subcategory') {
                    page += "/c";
                } else if (from == 'subdepartment_catalog') {
                    page += "/sd/catalog";
                }
            };
            page += ""; //convert to string

            var url = document.location.pathname.replace(/(\/p[0-9]+)?(\/c)?$/,page).replace(/\/resigilate(\/p[0-9]+)?/, '/resigilate' + page.replace(/\/c/, ''));
            document.location.href = url;
        });

        var noResults = $('.no-results-box2').length &gt; 0;
        var noResultsFallbackExists = noResults &amp;&amp; !($('.no-results-box2').hasClass('fallback'));
        if (noResultsFallbackExists) {
            $('.search-feedback-modal .close').hide();
        }

        $('.search-feedback-trigger .trigger-form-btn').click(function() {
            if ($(this).hasClass('disabled')) {
                    return false;
            }
            if ($(this).attr('data-value') == 'yes') {
                sendFeedback('yes');
                $(this).addClass('disabled');
            }
            else {
                $('.search-feedback-trigger').slideUp();
                $('.feedback-form-div').slideDown();
            }
        });

        $(".search-feedback-modal #search-details").focus(function() {
            $('.search-feedback-modal #search-details').removeClass('error-text');
            $('.search-feedback-modal #search-details').removeClass('error-field');
            $('.search-feedback-modal #search-details').removeAttr('placeholder');
        });

        $(".search-feedback-modal #search-email").focus(function() {
            $('.search-feedback-modal #search-email').removeClass('error-field');
        });
        $('.search-feedback-modal .submit').click(function(event){
            event.stopPropagation();
            sendFeedback('no');
            if (!$('.search-feedback-modal #search-details').hasClass('error-text')) {
                $('.search-feedback-trigger .trigger-form-btn').removeClass('disabled');
            }
        });

        $('.search-feedback-modal .close').click(function(){
            $('.feedback-form-div').slideUp('fast');
            $('.search-feedback-trigger').slideDown();
        });
    });

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

    function getViewport() {

        var viewPortWidth;
        var viewPortHeight;

        // the more standards compliant browsers (mozilla/netscape/opera/IE7) use window.innerWidth and window.innerHeight
        if (typeof window.innerWidth != 'undefined') {
            viewPortWidth = window.innerWidth,
                    viewPortHeight = window.innerHeight
        }

        // IE6 in standards compliant mode (i.e. with a valid doctype as the first line in the document)
        else if (typeof document.documentElement != 'undefined'
                &amp;&amp; typeof document.documentElement.clientWidth !=
                'undefined' &amp;&amp; document.documentElement.clientWidth != 0) {
            viewPortWidth = document.documentElement.clientWidth,
                    viewPortHeight = document.documentElement.clientHeight
        }

        // older versions of IE
        else {
            viewPortWidth = document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0].clientWidth,
                    viewPortHeight = document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0].clientHeight
        }
        return viewPortWidth + 'x' + viewPortHeight;
    }

    function createCookie(name,value,days) {
        if (days) {
            var date = new Date();
            date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
            var expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();
        }
        else var expires = "";
        document.cookie = name+"="+value+expires+"; path=/";
    }

    var screenResolution = window.screen.availWidth + 'x' + window.screen.availHeight;
    var viewPort = getViewport();

    createCookie('sr',screenResolution,365);
    createCookie('vp',viewPort,365);

    if($.cookie("_rsv") == null){
        var rsv = 1;
    } else {
        var rsv = eval($.cookie("_rsv")) + 1;
    }
    $.cookie("_rsv", rsv, { expires: 1, path:"/"});

    if($.cookie("_rsv") &gt;= 2){
        $.cookie("_rscd", 1, { expires: 1, path:"/"});
    }

    if($.cookie("_rsv") != null){
        var rsdc = eval($.cookie("_rscd")) + 1;
        $.cookie("_rsdc", rsdc, { expires: 3, path:"/"});
    }

    $(window).load(function(){
        if (typeof(GUI) !== "object"){
            $.getScript("https://s0emagst.akamaized.net/layout/ro/www/js/assetic/gui-55aec2d.js");
        }
        else{ 
            $(document).trigger('gui-init'); 
        }
        try {
            $.postLogin();
        }catch(e){
            console.info('PostLogin not defined');
        }

<script type="text/javascript">
    function get_browser_version(){
        var N=navigator.appName, ua=navigator.userAgent, tem;
        var M=ua.match(/(opera|chrome|safari|firefox|msie)\/?\s*(\.?\d+(\.\d+)*)/i);
        if(M &amp;&amp; (tem= ua.match(/version\/([\.\d]+)/i))!= null) M[2]= tem[1];
        M=M? [M[1], M[2]]: [N, navigator.appVersion, '-?'];
        return parseInt(M[1]);
    }
